# Request

```
POST /store_requester.php HTTP/1.1
Host: masterserver.naeu.heroesofnewerth.com
User-Agent: S2 Games/Heroes of Newerth/4.10.1.0/wac/x86_64
Accept: */*
Accept-Encoding: gzip,deflate
Content-Length: 153
Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded

account_id=9190611&category_id=0&request_code=0&page=0&cookie=f52479e4aff36eb692ce3e085c61a357&hostTime=9083995&displayAll=false&notPurchasable=false&bb
```

- `account_id`: The account ID of the user
- `currency:` The type of currency used
    - 0 for gold
    - 1 for silver
- `category_id`: An integer value mapping to an enum of the store tabs
    - 0 = Unset? Metadata?
    - 2 = Alt Avatars
    - 3 = Account Vanity -> Account Icons
    - 4 = Account Vanity -> Symbols
    - 5 = Game Vanity -> Announcers
    - 6 = Other
    - 7 = Bundles
    - 16 = Account Vanity -> Name Colors
    - 27 = Game Vanity -> Taunt
    - 57 = Game Vanity -> Couriers
    - 68 = Featured
    - 74 = Game Vanity -> Wards
    - 75 = Game Vanity -> Upgrades
    - 78 = Game Vanity -> TP Effects
    
- `request_code`: Specifies the type of request
    - 0 for unset
    - 1 for browse?
    - 2 for vault?
    - 4 for purchase/gift?
    - 5 open store to buy coins?
    - 6 for bundles?
    - 9 for promo unit quantity?
    - 10 for redeeming promo code
- `product_id`: The ID of the product being purchased
- `page`: 
- `cookie`: The cookie from the users authentication session.
- `hostTime`: The client hosttime, which must be forwarded back in the response.
- `displayAll`: Whether or not to display all content in this category??
- `notPurchasable`: I guess for non purchasable items??
- `bb`: Unclear, seems to be unset most the time?
- `santaTo`: Username when gifting to someone else
- `discount`: I guess some kind of discount flag?

```
    [timestamp] => 1649577290
    [accountIconsUnlocked] => 1
    [gameTokens] => 0
    [gamePasses] => 0
    [productEligibility] => 1769~19~0~0~0~1757;1759;1761;1765;1775|983~21~0~0~0~975;977;979;981|1771~27~1~0~0~1662;1688;1763;1767;1773|1966~33~1~0~0~2155;2156;2157;2158;2159;2160;2161;2162;2163;2164;2165;2166|2396~49~1~390~2500~|2390~50~0~390~2500~2271|2331~54~0~390~2500~2252|2394~55~0~390~2500~2202|2392~57~0~390~2500~2095|2095~58~0~195~1250~2392|2252~59~0~390~2500~2331|2328~60~1~390~2500~|2399~61~0~390~2500~2328|2342~77~0~390~2500~2173|2431~76~1~420~3500~|2173~78~1~390~2500~|2420~73~0~390~2500~1976|1976~74~0~390~2500~2420|2894~116~0~0~0~15;2623;2625;2644;2646;2648;2650;2652;2654;2761;2882|2091~110~0~390~2500~2526|2526~109~0~390~2500~2091|1623~108~1~0~0~1620|3298~163~0~0~0~3383;3384;3385;3386;3387;3388;3389;3390;3391;3392;3393;3394|1041~189~0~0~0~3411;3415;3421|4056~202~0~400~3000~4031;4064|3125~198~0~0~0~3887;3888;3889;3890;3891|4052~203~0~400~3000~4033;4035|4054~205~1~400~3000~|2194~210~0~400~3000~4118;4119|2333~211~0~400~3000~4117;4118|2246~212~0~400~3000~4119;4120|2307~213~0~400~3000~4117;4120|1279~214~0~200~500~4118;4119;4120|3111~215~0~390~2500~4117;4118;4119|1839~216~0~390~2500~4117;4119;4120|3364~217~0~390~2500~4117;4118;4120|1876~218~0~400~3000~4117;4118;4119;4120|4195~223~0~0~0~4177|4194~222~0~0~0~4175|4192~220~0~0~0~4171|4193~221~0~0~0~4173|3487~229~0~550~1000~4282|4282~230~0~550~9002~3487|2591~231~0~450~3500~2621|4531~243~0~0~0~4575|4533~242~0~0~0~4576|4599~246~0~0~0~4597|4594~248~0~420~3000~4596|4596~245~0~420~3000~4594|4590~244~0~0~0~4592|5290~309~0~0~0~5315|5334~310~0~0~0~5335|5331~311~0~0~0~5332|5337~312~0~0~0~5338|5340~314~0~0~0~5341
    [totalMMPoints] => 16465
    [vaultHighlight] => NULL
    [santas] => 4
    [santa_event_expiration] => 2072-06-22 10:15:59

```

- `responseCode`: `1` for success??
- `popupCode`: `-1` for no?
- `productPrices`: The gold coin price for the items
- `productNames`: The name of the items
- `productIDs`: The ID of the product in the store.
- `productAlreadyOwned`: A boolean indicating if the current user already owns the item or not (`1` for yes, `0` for no)
- `productIsBundle`: Whether or not the product is a bundleContents
- `productQuantity`: The available quantity of the item. Or `-1` if the item has no quantity specified.
- `totalPages`: The total number of pages of items available. Seems like it may be `6` or `10` for alt avatars?
- `totalPoints`: Account gold coin balance
- `productWebContent`: Path to web images for the item. e.g. `/images/heroes/127/icon_128.jpg` becomes `https://heroesofnewerth.com/images/heroes/127/icon_128.jpg`
- `productLocalContent`: Path to the local content for the item. e.g. `/heroes/chi/alt/icon.tga`
- `productDescription`: An optional text description for the item.
- `categoryID`: The category ID that these items belong to. 
    - 0 = Unset? Metadata?
    - 2 = Alt Avatars
    - 3 = Account Vanity -> Account Icons
    - 4 = Account Vanity -> Symbols
    - 5 = Game Vanity -> Announcers
    - 6 = Other
    - 7 = Bundles
    - 16 = Account Vanity -> Name Colors
    - 27 = Game Vanity -> Taunt
    - 57 = Game Vanity -> Couriers
    - 68 = Featured
    - 74 = Game Vanity -> Wards
    - 75 = Game Vanity -> Upgrades
    - 78 = Game Vanity -> TP Effects
- `currentPage`: The page index out of `totalPages` that corresponds to these results
- `errorCode`: Unknown? `0` if no error. Perhaps some value if various errors occur?
- `bundleContents`: Unset for this category.
- `selectedUpgrades`: Unset for this category.
- `requestHostTime`: The `hosttime` from the request. Must be forwarded to the response here to match.
- `tauntUnlocked`: Whether or not `taunt` is unlocked on this account.
- `tauntUnlockCostMMP`: The silver coin cost to unlock taunt.
- `customAccountIcon`: Unclear... Perhaps whether or not the account has a purchased `customAccountIcon` available.
- `customAccountIconCost`: Custom account icon cost in gold coins.
- `customAccountIconCostMMP`: Custom account icon cost in silver coins.
- `specialBundles`: Unclear... perhaps lists bundles that are for sale for the current item? Seems to be split by `~` and contain up to 5 items. `-1` for no item.
- `productCharges`: Unclear... Seems to be split by `~` and contains up to 6 items. `-1` for no item
- `productDurations`: Unclear... Seems to be split by `~` and contains up to 7 items. `-1` for no item.
- `productTimes`: Unclear... Seems to be split by `~` and contains up to 2 items. `-1` for no item.
- `purchasable`: A boolean indicating whether or not the item is purchasable. (`1` for yes, `0` for no)
 - `productPremium`: Unknown boolean. (`1` for yes, `0` for no)
- `premium_mmp_cost`: The cost of the item in silver coins.
- `productCodes`: The string product code corresponding to the item.
- `productStats`: Unclear. Seems to be 3 values separated by `~`. But I don't know what they mean. 
- `productEnhancements`: Any enhancements that come with the item. Separated by `~`. E.g. `paragon_pet~paragon_trail~empath_ability01_upgrade~empath_ability02_upgrade~empath_ability03_upgrade~empath_ability04_upgrade~empath_stat_track`
- `productEnhancementIDs`: The product ID for the enchancements. Separated by `~`.
- `chargesRemaining`: Unclear. Seems to be 3 values separated by `~`.
- `durationsRemaining`: Unclear.
- `timestamp`: Current UTC timestamp in seconds.
- `accountIconsUnlocked`: A boolean indicating whether or not account icons are unlocked. (I thought this was automatically unlocked?) Boolean. (`1` for yes, `0` for no)
- `gamePasses`: Garena only.
- `productEligibility`: No idea....
- `totalMMPoints`: The total amount of silver coins the account has.
- `vaultHighlight`: Unclear. Seems to be set to `NULL` for this category.
- `santas`: The number of store gift items remaining.
- `santa_event_expiration`: The expiration date timestamp for when the santa gifting event is over.
